        }

        const countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {"countries":["ES","MX","PH","TH","TR"]};

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

	<h2 class="pi-item pi-header pi-secondary-font pi-item-spacing pi-secondary-background"><span class="df-header">Devil Fruit</span></h2>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</h3>

	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a></div>

<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>"Kuma" redirects here. For other uses, see <a href="/wiki/Kuma_(Disambiguation)" class="mw-disambig" title="Kuma (Disambiguation)">Kuma (Disambiguation)</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>Bartholomew Kuma</b><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup> is a former <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a>, the former <a href="/wiki/King_(Title)" title="King (Title)">king</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Sorbet_Kingdom" title="Sorbet Kingdom">Sorbet Kingdom</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> and an <a href="/wiki/Officer" title="Officer">officer</a> and founding member of the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounty</a> of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload"></a></span>296,000,000.<sup id="cite_ref-c234_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c234-9">[9]</a></sup> As a <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">pirate</a>, Kuma sailed the <a href="/wiki/Blue_Sea" title="Blue Sea">seas</a> as a single-person pirate crew.<sup id="cite_ref-c1099_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1099-12">[12]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1100p17_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1100p17-13">[13]</a></sup> He is also the adoptive father of <a href="/wiki/Jewelry_Bonney" title="Jewelry Bonney">Jewelry Bonney</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup> daughter of his late friend and fellow revolutionary <a href="/wiki/Ginny" title="Ginny">Ginny</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1062_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1062-15">[15]</a></sup> Kuma is a member of the near-extinct special <a href="/wiki/Race" title="Race">race</a> known as the <a href="/wiki/Buccaneers" title="Buccaneers">Buccaneers</a>, inherited from his late father <a href="/wiki/Clapp" title="Clapp">Clapp</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup>
</p><p>Because of the lies the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> told the public, Kuma became feared as an extremely vicious pirate,<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup> earning himself the title <b>"Tyrant"</b>.<sup id="cite_ref-c474_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c474-6">[6]</a></sup> In exchange for curing Bonney of the deadly <a href="/wiki/Sapphire_Scales" title="Sapphire Scales">Sapphire Scales</a> <a href="/wiki/Diseases" title="Diseases">disease</a>, Kuma became a special type of <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">cyborg</a> known as a "<a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a>", developed by the <a href="/wiki/World" title="World">world</a> renowned <a href="/wiki/Scientist" title="Scientist">scientist</a> <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup> Once Vegapunk finished his modifications on Kuma, the Warlord was converted into the first complete Pacifista cyborg, with the serial <b>PX-0</b>, and mentally died in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-PX-0_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PX-0-4">[4]</a></sup> Vegapunk also <a href="/wiki/Cloning" title="Cloning">cloned</a> Kuma as <a href="/wiki/S-Bear" title="S-Bear">S-Bear</a>, one of the <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a> that were designed to replace the Warlords.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup>
</p><p>Kuma has been <a href="/wiki/Slavery" title="Slavery">enslaved</a> by the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a> twice in his lifetime:<sup id="cite_ref-c1095_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1095-21">[21]</a></sup> The first time was in his infancy until he escaped during the <a href="/wiki/God_Valley_Incident" title="God Valley Incident">God Valley Incident</a><sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup> and the second time in adulthood as punishment for the two years he spent protecting the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a><sup id="cite_ref-c908_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c908-23">[23]</a></sup> and lasted until his fellow revolutionaries freed him during the most recent <a href="/wiki/Levely" title="Levely">Levely</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1054_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1054-24">[24]</a></sup> 
</p><p>While Kuma was presented as a major antagonist during the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Arc" title="Thriller Bark Arc">Thriller Bark</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago_Arc" title="Sabaody Archipelago Arc">Sabaody Archipelago Arcs</a>, he was secretly an ally and his <a href="/wiki/Celestial_Dragon_Hit-and-Run_Incident" title="Celestial Dragon Hit-and-Run Incident">action of separating</a> the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> was ultimately done in their best interest, as it saved them from <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a> and helped the crew's <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Captain" title="Pirate Captain">captain</a> <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> realize that his crew was too weak to survive in the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>; thus, Kuma played a key role in the subsequent <a href="/wiki/Timeskip" title="Timeskip">timeskip</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup> In his mindless state, Kuma is a major antagonist in the <a href="/wiki/Marineford_Arc" title="Marineford Arc">Marineford Arc</a> where he took part in the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a> and sided with the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, along with most of the other Warlords,<sup id="cite_ref-Moria_at_Marineford_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moria_at_Marineford-26">[26]</a></sup> but he later becomes a major ally during the <a href="/wiki/Egghead_Arc" title="Egghead Arc">Egghead Arc</a> and an important figure behind its ongoings.
</p>

			<h3 class="trfc161__header-text">Quick Answers</h3>
		</div>
		<img class="trfc161-logo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/8941553e-df6a-4310-a080-b9da56fdcbdd" alt="fandom logo">
	</div>
	<div class="trfc161__groups">
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8207" data-revision-id="3">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the significance of Bartholomew Kuma's bounty in One Piece?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						In One Piece, a character's bounty is not just a reflection of their combat abilities, but also an indication of how much of a threat they pose to the World Government. Bartholomew Kuma, being one of the Seven Warlords of the Sea and a member of the Revolutionary Army, holds a significant bounty. This is due to his high combat abilities and his potential to cause considerable disruption to the government.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Community
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8208" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the story behind Kuma's flashback in the series?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						In the series, Bartholomew Kuma's flashback reveals his deep connection to the Revolutionary Army and his belief in Luffy's potential. Kuma was present during the training of Sabo, another key figure in the series. He also had a mysterious trip to the Goa Kingdom, where he observed Luffy's training from a distance. This sparked his interest in Luffy's growth and heroic deeds. Kuma's flashback also reveals his participation in an experiment conducted by Vegapunk, where he willingly gave up his own freedom and memories. These memories were manifested into a paw bubble for Vegapunk to study. Before his humanity was erased, Kuma declared his faith in Luffy and his crew to change the world.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8209" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What crucial information did Kuma reveal to Rayleigh?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						In a crucial moment, Bartholomew Kuma revealed to Rayleigh that he was an officer of the Revolutionary Army. His intentions were to help Luffy and his crew escape. Despite his seemingly antagonistic actions, Kuma's revelation showed that he was secretly an ally, and his actions were ultimately in the best interest of the Straw Hat Pirates. This revelation played a key role in the subsequent events and the development of the crew.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8211" data-revision-id="3">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">How does Kuma's adopted daughter play a role in saving the world?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Bartholomew Kuma adopted a daughter named Bonney. Despite not being related by blood, Kuma was a devoted father figure to Bonney, raising her with unconditional love and care. He was extremely protective of her, especially due to her health condition. Kuma even left the Revolutionary Army to keep watch over her. When the Sorbet Kingdom was set on fire, Kuma risked his own safety to rescue the victims, showing his heroic nature. Although Kuma had to leave Bonney due to an agreement with the World Government, his love and sacrifices for her were significant. Bonney, in turn, vouched for her father's reputation against false accusations by the Government, playing a role in saving the world by revealing the truth.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Community
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
	</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kuma is an enormous man, being 689 cm tall. He is the second tallest of the former Warlords (being three centimeters shorter than <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>) and is usually seen carrying a Bible. His hair is generally long and curly, and sometimes includes a pair of round protrusions resembling bear ears.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup> He wears glasses with clear-mirrored lenses which cover his <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">cybernetic</a> eyes. Prior to his conversion into a cyborg, his eyes were normal.
</p><p>His white hat and the dark blue fabric of his pants are covered in brown spots. His jacket contains a large white design reminiscent of a target crosshair or a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Coda_(music)#In_music_notation" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Coda (music)">coda sign</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-1">[1]</a></sup> There are also several white paw prints lining the bottom hem of his coat. He also has a long protruding chin. He bears the tattoo "PX-0" on the left side of the base of his throat, after the final touches were done on him becoming a complete <a href="/wiki/Cyborg" class="mw-redirect" title="Cyborg">cyborg</a> before the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>.
</p><p>In the anime, Kuma's hair and jacket are black, and his hat is gray with black paw-like prints. In the manga, <a href="/wiki/Eiichiro_Oda" title="Eiichiro Oda">Oda</a> originally intended for Kuma to have a completely different color scheme. Kuma's hair was shown to be brown, his jacket bright orange, and his hat yellow with green spots.<sup id="cite_ref-Kuma_True_Colors_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kuma_True_Colors-28">[28]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kuma_colors_2_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kuma_colors_2-29">[29]</a></sup> Later on the cover of <a href="/wiki/Chapter_532" title="Chapter 532">Chapter 532</a>, his coat was changed from orange to blue, though the rest of his design remained untouched.<sup id="cite_ref-Kuma_colors_3_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kuma_colors_3-30">[30]</a></sup> Later still, on <a href="/wiki/Volume_90" title="Volume 90">Volume 90</a>, Kuma's hair was changed to black, matching his depiction in the anime.<sup id="cite_ref-Kuma_colors_4_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kuma_colors_4-31">[31]</a></sup> In Unlimited Cruise, Kuma's jacket is brown.
</p><p>After the timeskip, Kuma's cybernetic armor has become heavily damaged, with a few weapons jutting out of his body, fruits of his mission to protect the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a> from attackers for two years. Due to his subsequent enslaving at <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a>, he wore rags similar to the ones <a href="/wiki/Jean_Bart" title="Jean Bart">Jean Bart</a> once wore when he was a slave, a collar and chain around his neck, has even more swords jutting out of his body as result of the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a> inflicting damage onto him for their own amusement, one of his cybernetic eyes is missing and he no longer holds his signature Bible. After he was freed from slavery, he went back to his original clothes and had all the swords removed from his body and it appears that his cybernetics have been repaired. After encountering <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</a> at Mary Geoise, a portion of Kuma's face was burned off by the fleet admiral's <a href="/wiki/Magu_Magu_no_Mi" title="Magu Magu no Mi">magma</a>.
</p><p>Having been a <a href="/wiki/Slavery" title="Slavery">slave</a> to the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a> as a child and in adulthood, Kuma should have been branded with the Hoof of the Flying Dragon,<sup id="cite_ref-hoof_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hoof-32">[32]</a></sup> though it is unknown where it is on his body.
</p><p>As a child, Kuma's head was shaved, thus lacking his bear ears, glasses, and <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">cybernetic enhancements</a> he received later on. He was already bigger than average children and usually wore tattered clothing.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup> As a baby and a four-year old, he had blushy cheeks, which he inherited from his mother.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallery">Gallery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Main_Series">Main Series</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 132px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Kuma_Wanted_Poster.png/revision/latest?cb=20231126150200" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Wanted Poster" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="97" height="110" data-image-name="Kuma Wanted Poster.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Wanted_Poster.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/28/Kuma_Wanted_Poster.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/97?cb=20231126150200" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kuma's first known wanted poster.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 132px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Bartholomew_Kuma_Hatless.png/revision/latest?cb=20240220050644" class="image"><img alt="Bartholomew Kuma Hatless" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="105" data-image-name="Bartholomew Kuma Hatless.png" data-image-key="Bartholomew_Kuma_Hatless.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Bartholomew_Kuma_Hatless.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20240220050644" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kuma without his hat on.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kuma is a tragic and complex individual who has experienced major turmoils and sacrifices throughout his life that have greatly altered his overall character. While kind and self-sacrificing at heart, his struggles and choices have ultimately led him to a point where he can no longer be considered a live human being with free will. 
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">When I was a boy I wanted to be a hero. Someone who could save people from suffering and grant them their freedom. Just like the legendary warrior of liberation <a href="/wiki/Nika" title="Nika">Nika</a>.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Kuma telling Bonney about how he has always looked up to Nika.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
During his early childhood, Kuma was a pretty cheerful kid before his subsequent enslavement and the death of his parents broke him into utter despair. That said, the buccaneer folk tales about the legend of <a href="/wiki/Nika" title="Nika">Nika</a> his father <a href="/wiki/Clapp" title="Clapp">Clapp</a> told him gave Kuma happiness, hope and a hero figure to idolize amidst his life as a slave. Kuma has since grown into someone who seeks to liberate people from oppression by corrupt authorities, much like the figure of Nika, due to having been an oppressed victim himself. He has similarly shared this story with his daughter Bonney, in order to provide the same hope to her that his father once did to him. As a result of his worship of Nika and likely love for his deceased father, Kuma tends to break into dancing to the Rhythm of Liberation whenever the topic of his idol comes up.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2f/Kuma_in_Prayer.png/revision/latest?cb=20231030140610" class="image"><img alt="Kuma in Prayer" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="188" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma in Prayer.png" data-image-key="Kuma_in_Prayer.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2f/Kuma_in_Prayer.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231030140610"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2f/Kuma_in_Prayer.png/revision/latest?cb=20231030140610" class="image"><img alt="Kuma in Prayer" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2f/Kuma_in_Prayer.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231030140610" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="188" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma in Prayer.png" data-image-key="Kuma_in_Prayer.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2f/Kuma_in_Prayer.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231030140610"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_in_Prayer.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma praying for the lost lives of the Native Hunting Competition.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Because he was raised in a church, Kuma is deeply religious and tends to pray for long periods, which is reflected nowadays by his signature bible and aforementioned devotion to Nika. Even after escaping slavery, young Kuma was extremely kind and forgiving, willing to use his powers to treat the wounds of even those who would bully him, never showing any sort of grudge or resentment against said people. He would eventually grow up into an altruistic pastor, always helping those in need even if at the expense of his own life and physical well-being.
</p><p>In spite of his epithet implying a violent personality, Kuma was an extraordinarily gentle man, whose kindness earned him great respect from his fellow Revolutionaries.<sup id="cite_ref-c485_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c485-35">[35]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-sabaody_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sabaody-36">[36]</a></sup> That said, there was a period after the abduction of his friend and romantic interest <a href="/wiki/Ginny" title="Ginny">Ginny</a> when Kuma became a more audacious and aggressive soldier who would recklessly charge into battle by himself, often exhausting himself as a result. It was only after making contact with Ginny again and finding an infant Bonney near her dead mother that Kuma would revert back to his original mellow persona.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Kuma_Accepts_Fate.png/revision/latest?cb=20231212184231" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Accepts Fate" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="172" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma Accepts Fate.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Accepts_Fate.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Kuma_Accepts_Fate.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231212184231"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Kuma_Accepts_Fate.png/revision/latest?cb=20231212184231" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Accepts Fate" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Kuma_Accepts_Fate.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231212184231" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="172" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma Accepts Fate.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Accepts_Fate.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Kuma_Accepts_Fate.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231212184231"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_Accepts_Fate.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma gratefully accepting his fate in order to have Bonney cured.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kuma was a very loving father to his adopted daughter, Bonney, having raised her out of love and respect for Ginny.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup> Indeed, Bonney vouched that her father's reputation as an evil tyrant was falsely advertised by the Government and that he is in fact, an extremely kind individual.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup> When King Bekori set fire to the southern side of Sorbet Kingdom to massacre the poor citizens by burning them alive in their homes, Kuma risked his own safety in an attempt to rescue the victims by braving the raging inferno, which led to him being elected King by Sorbet's population due to his great benevolence and selflessness. By Kuma's own admission, he is a pacifist by nature, although one willing to fight back, if necessary, in order to maintain peace.
</p><p>Even after taking part in the <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> project and becoming an agent for the World Government, Kuma kept most of his original personality and positive qualities intact for a brief time, but still had to maintain an intimidating image towards pirates due to his position as a Warlord of the Sea, which likely further contributed to his image as a loyal "government dog" among those who did not know him (even other Warlords, such as <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>). During this time, he consistently acted calm and composed; he generally did not speak much unless it was absolutely necessary and maintained a stoic disposition at all times. While he would still exhibit some unique quirks of his own, like using the word "target" in his sentences or asking people where they would like to go on a holiday before sending them away with his <a href="/wiki/Nikyu_Nikyu_no_Mi" title="Nikyu Nikyu no Mi">Devil Fruit</a> ability (a habit that he seemingly picked up from his time as a stay-at-home father),<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup> Kuma always presented himself as a serious, enigmatic person, keeping very few people aware of his true motivations. Despite earning himself such an unflattering reputation, Kuma's usual mercy and empathy were put on display when he honored and respected <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a>'s choice for putting his own life on the line for his captain's safety. Kuma was willing to give the swordsman a chance to save <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>, in spite of conflicting with the mission that he was assigned.
</p>

<p><br>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Bartholomew_Kuma_Talks_to_Rayleigh.png/revision/latest?cb=20230124130004" class="image"><img alt="Bartholomew Kuma Talks to Rayleigh" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bartholomew Kuma Talks to Rayleigh.png" data-image-key="Bartholomew_Kuma_Talks_to_Rayleigh.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Bartholomew_Kuma_Talks_to_Rayleigh.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230124130004"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Bartholomew_Kuma_Talks_to_Rayleigh.png/revision/latest?cb=20230124130004" class="image"><img alt="Bartholomew Kuma Talks to Rayleigh" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Bartholomew_Kuma_Talks_to_Rayleigh.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230124130004" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bartholomew Kuma Talks to Rayleigh.png" data-image-key="Bartholomew_Kuma_Talks_to_Rayleigh.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c2/Bartholomew_Kuma_Talks_to_Rayleigh.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230124130004"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bartholomew_Kuma_Talks_to_Rayleigh.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma delivers his message to Rayleigh.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite being perceived as the most dutiful of the Seven Warlords of the Sea, Kuma was never really loyal to the World Government's cause and frequently acted against their interests through subtle, deniable manners. Kuma's loyalty similarly did not extend to the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c513_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c513-40">[40]</a></sup> Because of that, Kuma did not hesitate to lie to <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> when it came to his ambiguous victory over the Straw Hat Pirates at <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>, as no one could prove that he was in fact helping them in secret. Most of Kuma's obedience towards his superiors seemingly came from their hold over his daughter Bonney, as a consequence of the terms he had to agree with the government to save her life. In spite of said terms being incredibly damaging to Kuma himself, he gladly accepted them, citing that Bonney's life was his ultimate priority.
</p><p>Outside his daughter, Kuma's sole loyalty remains towards the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a>, of which he still considers himself to be part of despite his current position as a Warlord and prior resignation from the rebel group, even showing a desire to return and fight alongside his former comrades once more. Kuma has admired the efforts of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a> since the latter's time as the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Freedom_Fighters" title="Freedom Fighters">Freedom Fighters</a>, believing the group were akin to heroes who helped people around the world. It is also heavily implied that Luffy being the son of Dragon was the main reason for Kuma's continued assistance of the Straw Hat Pirates.
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
