<p><br>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fb/Bartholomew_Kuma_Pacifista_Programming.png/revision/latest?cb=20230124130302" class="image"><img alt="Bartholomew Kuma Pacifista Programming" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bartholomew Kuma Pacifista Programming.png" data-image-key="Bartholomew_Kuma_Pacifista_Programming.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fb/Bartholomew_Kuma_Pacifista_Programming.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230124130302"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fb/Bartholomew_Kuma_Pacifista_Programming.png/revision/latest?cb=20230124130302" class="image"><img alt="Bartholomew Kuma Pacifista Programming" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fb/Bartholomew_Kuma_Pacifista_Programming.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230124130302" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bartholomew Kuma Pacifista Programming.png" data-image-key="Bartholomew_Kuma_Pacifista_Programming.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fb/Bartholomew_Kuma_Pacifista_Programming.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230124130302"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bartholomew_Kuma_Pacifista_Programming.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma getting his brain and free will reprogrammed.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At present, with Kuma's Pacifista modifications having been completed, he completely lost his free will, personality and memory in order to ensure his reliability and continuing services towards the World Government. In this stage, Kuma shares the same mindless intelligence of his fellow Pacifista models, only recognizing individuals as either enemies or allies to the government. <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Doflamingo</a> refers to the original personality as being "dead",<sup id="cite_ref-PX-0_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PX-0-4">[4]</a></sup> though it was later revealed that Kuma and Dr. <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a> (the man responsible for his cybernetic implants) made a secret deal to allow for Kuma to have a temporary relapse by rendering his final "free thought" as defending the Thousand Sunny. After that, Kuma was relegated to working as a slave-to-rent and obeying the demands of the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a> without question. After being freed by the Revolutionaries, he no longer appeared to have any sort of humanity left within him.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup>
</p><p>A few days after Kuma was rescued by the Revolutionaries, <a href="/wiki/Jaygarcia_Saturn" title="Jaygarcia Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</a> activated a failsafe that he demanded Vegapunk install in Kuma; while Saturn's intent was for Vegapunk to install a bomb in Kuma, Vegapunk instead merely designed the switch to completely shut off Kuma's body and mind, effectively rendering him lifeless. During the same time, possibly in response to being programmed to shut down, enough of Kuma's personality reawakened for him to instinctively travel to his daughter at <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a> and protect her from Saturn.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup> Ever since, despite remaining incapable of normal speech, he has shown bits of emotions such as embracing Bonney after saving her, reacting to Luffy taking on the appearance of Nika, listening intently to Bonney's speech to Saturn as she defeated him while taking on Nika's form, smiling after she defeated him, and smiling while holding Bonney on the <a href="/wiki/Great_Eirik" title="Great Eirik">Great Eirik</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup> While he is still a far cry from the man he used to be, these displays have suggested that he may once again be able to feel and express emotion as he once did.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family_and_Friends">Family and Friends</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Parents">Parents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Kuma%27s_Family_Enslaved.png/revision/latest?cb=20231101234611" class="image"><img alt="Kuma's Family Enslaved" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma's Family Enslaved.png" data-image-key="Kuma%27s_Family_Enslaved.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Kuma%27s_Family_Enslaved.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231101234611"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Kuma%27s_Family_Enslaved.png/revision/latest?cb=20231101234611" class="image"><img alt="Kuma's Family Enslaved" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Kuma%27s_Family_Enslaved.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231101234611" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma's Family Enslaved.png" data-image-key="Kuma%27s_Family_Enslaved.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Kuma%27s_Family_Enslaved.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231101234611"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma%27s_Family_Enslaved.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma with his enslaved parents.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kuma and his parents loved each other very much. His father <a href="/wiki/Clapp" title="Clapp">Clapp</a> wanted to protect him from slavery by the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a> because of his Buccaneer heritage. Despite Kuma feeling very sad about his mother's death and enduring hardships as a slave, Clapp always cheered him up by telling him about the Warrior <a href="/wiki/Nika" title="Nika">Nika</a> and that they would be rescued by him. It is because of his father's words that Kuma wanted to become a hero and help slaves someday.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jewelry_Bonney">Jewelry Bonney</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d9/Kuma_%26_Bonney_Dancing.png/revision/latest?cb=20231101234544" class="image"><img alt="Kuma &amp; Bonney Dancing" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="205" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma &amp; Bonney Dancing.png" data-image-key="Kuma_%26_Bonney_Dancing.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d9/Kuma_%26_Bonney_Dancing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231101234544"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d9/Kuma_%26_Bonney_Dancing.png/revision/latest?cb=20231101234544" class="image"><img alt="Kuma &amp; Bonney Dancing" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d9/Kuma_%26_Bonney_Dancing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231101234544" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="205" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma &amp; Bonney Dancing.png" data-image-key="Kuma_%26_Bonney_Dancing.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d9/Kuma_%26_Bonney_Dancing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231101234544"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_%26_Bonney_Dancing.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma teaching Bonney about Nika.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kuma is <a href="/wiki/Jewelry_Bonney" title="Jewelry Bonney">Bonney</a>'s adoptive father, and the only family member she has left. The two of them had a very loving relationship, as Bonney had fond memories of her childhood with him. Though not related by blood, Kuma was an extremely devoted father figure, doing his best to raise Bonney with unconditional love and care in honor of her mother Ginny, being emotionally moved by her growth since she was an infant.
</p><p>Because of Bonney's <a href="/wiki/Sapphire_Scales" title="Sapphire Scales">condition</a>, Kuma was very protective of her, making sure to do anything in his power to prevent her disease from getting worse, leaving the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a> in order to keep watch over her. Still, he wished to find a cure for his adopted daughter's disease and then travel around the world with her. The reveal that Bonney would likely die before she could enjoy life, however, left him heartbroken.
</p><p>Kuma became a pirate in order to find someone who could treat Bonney's disease. He eventually met with Dr. Vegapunk, who claimed that he could do exactly so. Still, because the World Government became aware of his attempts to strike an illegal deal with Vegapunk, he had to agree to additional terms that essentially sacrificed his own body and mind for the government's use. Kuma gladly accepted this and did not regret his decision, having stated that he would even deal with the devil if it meant allowing Bonney a chance to live.
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">One last thing Bonney...you're probably sick of hearing me saying this, but...I love you so much. I'll be sure to write again soon.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— One of Kuma's many written letters to Bonney.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">[46]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
While Kuma acted as a Warlord, he would often send loving letters to Bonney. Unbeknown to him though, his letters were all intercepted and destroyed by <a href="/wiki/Cipher_Pol" title="Cipher Pol">Cipher Pol</a> agent <a href="/wiki/Alpha" title="Alpha">Alpha</a>, who was in charge of Bonney's "well-being" following his deal with the government. Because Kuma's letters never reached her due to Alpha's meddling, Bonney would be left frustrated and disappointed throughout her recovery period, yet she never stopped believing in her father, deciding to leave Sorbet and become a pirate in order to reunite with him.
</p><p>While Kuma was aware that Bonney had set out to sea specifically to reunite with him, he preferred to keep himself away from her in order to honor his prior deal with the World Government and avoid jeopardazing Bonney's own safety. Kuma would keep thinking over Bonney until his last moments of free will, requesting Vegapunk to wish her a happy birthday in his stead, knowing that he would be unable to do so after his modifications were completed.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Kuma_Hugs_Bonney.png/revision/latest?cb=20240918024047" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Hugs Bonney" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma Hugs Bonney.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Hugs_Bonney.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Kuma_Hugs_Bonney.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240918024047"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Kuma_Hugs_Bonney.png/revision/latest?cb=20240918024047" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Hugs Bonney" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Kuma_Hugs_Bonney.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240918024047" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma Hugs Bonney.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Hugs_Bonney.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/55/Kuma_Hugs_Bonney.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240918024047"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_Hugs_Bonney.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma reunites with Bonney.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Bonney, who was unaware of the arrangements her father had to make to save her life, shows an intense rage towards the World Government for enslaving him and allowing him to suffer abuse at the hands of the World Nobles. Because she is so devoted to her father, Bonney has major reservations over witnessing the <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> getting attacked, due to their <a href="/wiki/Cloning" title="Cloning">resemblance</a> to Kuma. When Bonney discovered the true reason behind Kuma's conversion into a Pacifista, she broke down in tears and was on the verge of losing the will to live. When she was about to be killed by Saturn, Kuma, however, miraculously managed to reach her in time and struck Saturn, embracing Bonney with a warm hug, after four years of being separated, but unable to speak. Kuma also shows his smile to Bonney for beating up Saturn in order to repel the Elder. After escaping Egghead, Kuma and Bonney are happy when they are together again. 
</p>
<h4><span id="Sorbet.27s_Citizens"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Sorbet's_Citizens">Sorbet's Citizens</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As a priest, Kuma was beloved by the elderly population of Sorbet, particularly those who lived in village near his church. Every weekend, Kuma would use his abilities to take their pain away to absorb them himself later. Because the elders were physically unable to contribute much to Sorbet's Heavenly Tribute, they relied on Kuma's "miracles" in order to remain healthy and fit, as otherwise they would be imprisoned by King Bekori's draconian policies. 
</p><p>Even after becoming a Revolutionary, Kuma would still occasionally return to Sorbet to watch over his elderly friends. The elders also assisted Kuma in raising an infant Bonney, giving him tips about how to do so and directly taking care of her while he went out for revolutionary missions.
</p><p>Kuma was also friends with <a href="/wiki/Gyogyo" title="Gyogyo">Gyogyo</a> and other younger citizens of similar age to his, having befriended them shortly after escaping slavedom when he was nine. Kuma and Ginny mostly lived through food donations provided by them. As Kuma prepared to have his personality erased, Gyogyo was one of the people he recalled.
</p><p>After deposing of Bekori six years ago and saving the country from his destructive policies, Kuma was elected King by the population of Sorbet. Despite having no interest in ruling the kingdom, Kuma still accepted the role as he did not feel like going against popular demand.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bulldog">Bulldog</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Bulldog" title="Bulldog">Bulldog</a> was Kuma's advisor during the latter's tenure as king, taking care of Sorbet's political matters while Kuma remained working in his church. As a former king himself, Bulldog's own leadership qualities were trusted by Kuma.
</p><p>When Kuma had to abandon Sorbet in order to confront Bekori, he had no problems entrusting the country and his own daughter Bonney to Bulldog's care.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Revolutionaries">Revolutionaries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Revolutionary_Army_Drinking.png/revision/latest?cb=20231127022052" class="image"><img alt="Revolutionary Army Drinking" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="171" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Revolutionary Army Drinking.png" data-image-key="Revolutionary_Army_Drinking.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Revolutionary_Army_Drinking.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231127022052"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Revolutionary_Army_Drinking.png/revision/latest?cb=20231127022052" class="image"><img alt="Revolutionary Army Drinking" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Revolutionary_Army_Drinking.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231127022052" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="171" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Revolutionary Army Drinking.png" data-image-key="Revolutionary_Army_Drinking.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Revolutionary_Army_Drinking.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231127022052"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Revolutionary_Army_Drinking.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma drinking with the Revolutionary Army.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Prior to receiving his final modifications, Kuma was a loyal member of the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a>, having been one of the organization's original founders alongside his comrades Dragon and <a href="/wiki/Emporio_Ivankov" title="Emporio Ivankov">Ivankov</a>. Even after resigning from the army due to Bonney's health, Kuma never stopped thinking of himself as a revolutionary soldier.
</p><p>Kuma is deeply respected by his fellow revolutionaries as <a href="/wiki/Sabo" title="Sabo">Sabo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Morley" title="Morley">Morley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Karasu" title="Karasu">Karasu</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Lindbergh" title="Lindbergh">Lindbergh</a> planned to liberate Kuma from his torturous slavery during their infiltration of <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a>, which they successfully did and escaped with him. Sabo and <a href="/wiki/Koala" title="Koala">Koala</a> in particular did not understand at first why Kuma became an agent of the government, unaware of the special circumstances surrounding him that led to his status as a Warlord.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When he was around 22, Kuma became aware of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a> through newspaper articles. He already admired Dragon's <a href="/wiki/Freedom_Fighters" title="Freedom Fighters">Freedom Fighters</a> at the time and was more than happy to follow him, especially after Sorbet's liberation from King <a href="/wiki/Bekori" title="Bekori">Bekori</a>'s tyranny. Dragon, meanwhile, became aware of Kuma through Ivankov's recommendations.
</p><p>Dragon guaranteed to Kuma that joining the organization was the right choice to make, and Kuma would prove himself to be a highly effective asset for the organization. Even after Kuma left the army in order to spend more time with Bonney due to her illness, Dragon was not against his decision and encouraged him to live without regrets. He also promised Kuma that he would try to contact any doctors who could go on to help his daughter.
</p><p>Kuma also had knowledge of Luffy being Dragon's son<sup id="cite_ref-c485_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c485-35">[35]</a></sup> (something that even Ivankov was unaware of until he met the boy). Back during an operation at Goa, Kuma happened to see Dragon watching over a boy at <a href="/wiki/Foosha_Village" title="Foosha Village">Foosha Village</a> and deduced that they could have been related, asking his superior if there was any truth to that. While Dragon did imply Kuma's suspicions were correct, he refused to outright confirm them, with Kuma deciding to drop the subject due to noticing Dragon's discomfort. Kuma subsequently spared the Straw Hats' lives on two occasions, as well as guarding their ship for 2 years from the likes of pirates and Marines, due to their common connection.
</p><p>Though Kuma was working with the Revolutionary Army in secret as a <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord</a> (although he refused to speak with them for unknown reasons), his final modification into a full <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> now places him fully under the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>'s control. Dragon is seemingly not aware of Kuma's deal with the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>, but respected Kuma's wishes to not be followed or talked with before losing his free will for good. 
</p><p>After Kuma was recovered from his second enslavement by the revolutionaries, he identified Dragon as only his "master" due to his new programming overriding his old personality.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ginny">Ginny</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Ginny_Defending_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20231029201807" class="image"><img alt="Ginny Defending Kuma" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="204" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginny Defending Kuma.png" data-image-key="Ginny_Defending_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Ginny_Defending_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029201807"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Ginny_Defending_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20231029201807" class="image"><img alt="Ginny Defending Kuma" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Ginny_Defending_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029201807" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="204" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginny Defending Kuma.png" data-image-key="Ginny_Defending_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cb/Ginny_Defending_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231029201807"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginny_Defending_Kuma.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ginny defending Kuma from bullies.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Ginny" title="Ginny">Ginny</a> was Kuma's fellow slave and romantic interest who had met at God Valley. It was thanks to Ginny's ingenuity that Kuma was given an opportunity to escape his masters' and the <a href="/wiki/Native_Hunting_Competition" title="Native Hunting Competition">Native Hunting Competition</a>.
</p><p>When Kuma returned to the Sorbet Kingdom, Ginny decided to stay with him since she had no idea yet of what to do in life. She went on to live happily with Kuma, having full meals and living through honest work after leaving their slavedom behind. She was also protective of Kuma against bullies and acted as his "big sis", being four years his senior. As adults, Ginny would often chastise Kuma for his self-sacrifices regarding the elderly population of Sorbet, taking care of him afterwards every time he took in their pain.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Kuma_Mourning_Ginny_Death.png/revision/latest?cb=20240419001155" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Mourning Ginny Death" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="64" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma Mourning Ginny Death.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Mourning_Ginny_Death.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Kuma_Mourning_Ginny_Death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240419001155"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Kuma_Mourning_Ginny_Death.png/revision/latest?cb=20240419001155" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Mourning Ginny Death" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Kuma_Mourning_Ginny_Death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240419001155" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="64" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma Mourning Ginny Death.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Mourning_Ginny_Death.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/14/Kuma_Mourning_Ginny_Death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240419001155"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_Mourning_Ginny_Death.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma mourns Ginny's death.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While Kuma had mutual feelings for Ginny and enjoyed having her at his side, he refused to accept her marriage proposal due to what happened with his mother, who was enslaved solely for having a buccaneer husband. Despite this, Ginny still remained loyal to Kuma and was smitten with him even during their time in the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a>. After Ginny was captured by the World Government, Kuma became deeply enraged, recklessly charging into battle alone. After two years, when Ginny contacted Kuma to tell her that she was dying and proclaimed her love for him, he immediately headed for the chapel they grew up together in, knowing she would be there. After finding her dead, Kuma profusely wept for her as he reminisced of all the time they spent together and buried her, promising to raise her daughter in her stead.
</p><p>Ginny frequently referred to Kuma as "Kuma-chi".
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Emporio_Ivankov">Emporio Ivankov</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Kuma_and_Ivankov_confrontation.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206162352" class="image"><img alt="Kuma and Ivankov confrontation" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="159" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma and Ivankov confrontation.png" data-image-key="Kuma_and_Ivankov_confrontation.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Kuma_and_Ivankov_confrontation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20141206162352"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Kuma_and_Ivankov_confrontation.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206162352" class="image"><img alt="Kuma and Ivankov confrontation" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Kuma_and_Ivankov_confrontation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20141206162352" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="159" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma and Ivankov confrontation.png" data-image-key="Kuma_and_Ivankov_confrontation.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Kuma_and_Ivankov_confrontation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20141206162352"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_and_Ivankov_confrontation.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ivankov and Kuma confronting each other at Marineford.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Kuma was nine years old, he first met a fifteen-year-old <a href="/wiki/Emporio_Ivankov" title="Emporio Ivankov">Ivankov</a> at <a href="/wiki/God_Valley" title="God Valley">God Valley</a> as both were slaves at the time. They both worked together to successfully escape the Native Hunting Competition, with Ivankov praising Kuma for his actions of humility and self-sacrifice during their plan. Kuma's use of the Nikyu Nikyu no Mi also led Ivankov to dub Kuma as having the <b>Hands of Liberation</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">解放の手</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kaihō no Te</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>. When they parted ways during their childhood, Kuma told Ivankov he would never forget his face as long as he lives.
</p><p>Ivankov later recommended Kuma as a possible recruit for Dragon's freedom fighting goals, with the two freeing Kuma from imprisonment following King Bekori's fall. The two would go on to become close as Revolutionary comrades later on in life, with Ivankov knowing of Kuma's deep hatred for the World Government. 
</p><p>When Ivankov saw Kuma at the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, the former was shocked to see that Kuma was no longer the man he once was, which led to them confronting each other. Ivankov also claims Kuma fears him to some extent and was set to make him remember that cyborg or not.<sup id="cite_ref-c558_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c558-47">[47]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/59/Kuma_Vs_Straw_Hats.png/revision/latest?cb=20231227033854" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Vs Straw Hats" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma Vs Straw Hats.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Vs_Straw_Hats.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/59/Kuma_Vs_Straw_Hats.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231227033854"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/59/Kuma_Vs_Straw_Hats.png/revision/latest?cb=20231227033854" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Vs Straw Hats" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/59/Kuma_Vs_Straw_Hats.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231227033854" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma Vs Straw Hats.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Vs_Straw_Hats.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/59/Kuma_Vs_Straw_Hats.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231227033854"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_Vs_Straw_Hats.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma overshadowing the Straw Hat Pirates.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kuma believes the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> are destined to save and bring justice to the world somehow, having acknowledged the many impressive, if not miraculous, feats the crew has pulled since they began their pirate career all the way back in the <a href="/wiki/East_Blue" title="East Blue">East Blue</a>, starting with <a href="/wiki/Arlong" title="Arlong">Arlong</a>'s defeat. Since then, he has accompanied their growth through the news, although never getting to meet them personally until the events of the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Arc" title="Thriller Bark Arc">Thriller Bark Arc</a>. He first met <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> and was courteous enough to not engage her in battle, merely questioning her about the nature of Luffy and Ace's relationship.
</p><p>After Kuma witnessed Luffy defeating <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>, he reported it to the World Government, and they ordered Kuma to kill all witnesses on <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>, including the Straw Hats. As most of the pirates were already exhausted from fighting Moria, Kuma had little challenge in finishing them off. After a brief fight with <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a>, Kuma offered to spare everyone else if they allowed him to take Luffy alone, as that was his primary mission to begin with. They refused and Kuma, seemingly disappointed that he had to kill them all, attacked his opponents with an Ursus Shock, knocking out most of the Straw Hats. 
</p><p>Before Kuma could take Luffy away, Zoro, who was still conscious, attacked one last time and learned about Kuma's cybernetic nature. Seeing no other way to win as Kuma was still stronger and had the upper hand, Zoro offered to trade his life for Luffy's, with Sanji attempting to do the same only for Zoro to stop him. With his own honor at stake, Kuma agreed to Zoro's terms and subjugated him into experiencing the pain Luffy endured throughout his fight against Moria. Acknowledging Zoro's loyalty, Kuma even mused about Dragon having a good son with a loyal crew.
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">That is not true!! This is just the level of the New World. It is still too soon for the likes of your crew!! Don't come here yet. One day in the future... you will be the man... who saves the world.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup></td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
After the events of Thriller Bark, Kuma witnessed another <a href="/wiki/Celestial_Dragon_Hit-and-Run_Incident" title="Celestial Dragon Hit-and-Run Incident">outrageous incident</a> where the World Noble <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Charlos</a> was physically assaulted by Luffy at the <a href="/wiki/Human_Auctioning_House" title="Human Auctioning House">Human Auctioning House</a>. This was enough to spur Kuma into saving the crew's life once more, helping them escape Admiral <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sentomaru" title="Sentomaru">Sentomaru</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sabaody_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sabaody-36">[36]</a></sup> He gave Luffy one final farewell before sending him to <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Lily" title="Amazon Lily">Amazon Lily</a> and losing his free will to the <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> project's finalization. Kuma's motives for this unexpected action were clear: the crew was not ready for the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a> yet and needed to become far stronger.
</p><p>He also made a deal with <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a> to program him to protect the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a> until a Straw Hat member returned. Franky told the other Straw Hats that they owed a debt to Kuma, although he noted the next time they would meet, Kuma would be a heartless, human weapon. When Kuma arrived at Egghead to save Bonney, Franky decided to act on this debt for helping the Straw Hats two years ago at Sabaody, by protecting him against Saturn along with Sanji.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">

  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">His actions have really moved me. I know Nika is meant to be a legend, but...it'd be great if there really was a warrior out there, putting smiles on people's faces, using the rhythm of liberation...the rhythm I taught Bonney. And if there is a hero out there that will change these seas one day...I believe it'll be him.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>

  </td>

<p><br>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Kuma_Moved_By_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20231227045054" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Moved By Luffy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="185" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma Moved By Luffy.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Moved_By_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Kuma_Moved_By_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231227045054"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Kuma_Moved_By_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20231227045054" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Moved By Luffy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Kuma_Moved_By_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231227045054" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="185" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma Moved By Luffy.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Moved_By_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Kuma_Moved_By_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231227045054"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_Moved_By_Luffy.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma placing his hopes in Luffy.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kuma knows a lot about <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, as he was aware that <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a> and <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a> were his adoptive brother and biological father, respectively, despite both relationships not being public matter at the time.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c485_35-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c485-35">[35]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Luffy_is_Dragon's_son_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Luffy_is_Dragon's_son-51">[51]</a></sup> Back when he was still a revolutionary, Kuma suspected that Dragon may have had a family back in the <a href="/wiki/Goa_Kingdom" title="Goa Kingdom">Goa Kingdom</a> during a trip there, something that Dragon only indirectly confirmed and refused to elaborate further, which Kuma understood as an sensitive topic to talk about with his superior. 
</p><p>Around the time Luffy was 16, Kuma once headed to <a href="/wiki/Mt._Colubo" title="Mt. Colubo">Mt. Colubo</a> in order to confirm his suspicions about Dragon, leading him to find Luffy and observe his training from afar. Ever since then, Kuma has been accompanying the boy's growth and heroic deeds through news and bounty posters, while also pondering about his similarities to Nika, as a person who similarly opposed the World Government through his <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi">rubber abilities</a>. 
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Dragon, Iva... Please forgive me for vanishing without a word. I will leave behind the mark of my existence in Bonney and the future of this boy.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup></td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
Kuma later witnessed Luffy breaking the greatest taboo by striking a Celestial Dragon to save his friend <a href="/wiki/Hatchan" title="Hatchan">Hatchan</a>, which led the Warlord to hold high hopes for the boy and his potential to save the world, thus Kuma worked to secretly save Luffy and his crew by teleporting them away to safety from Kizaru and subsequently the New World.
</p><p>By the time he entered the final phase of his Pacifista modification process, Kuma was fully convinced Luffy had all the necessary qualities to change the world due to his selfless determination to help people from tyranny, much akin to his idol Nika, thus he requested Vegapunk to program him with a mission to protect the Thousand Sunny as a last favor to the Straw Hats after losing his free will.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup> Two years later at the island of <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a>, Kuma would witness Luffy again while in his <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_5_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 5 Techniques">Nika form</a>, having his belief on the boy confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Roronoa_Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kuma admitted that he was impressed with <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a> still being alive following the events at Thriller Bark, as he genuinely did not expect the swordsman to survive taking Luffy's own pain (admitting the latter's pain was enough to him unconscious).<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup> Zoro, too, recognized and respected Kuma’s strength, admitting that he was only alive because of the other’s honor and mercy.<sup id="cite_ref-c512_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c512-56">[56]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government_and_Marines">World Government and Marines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kuma has always had a hostile relationship with the World Government, having been enslaved by them at a young age solely for being born to a <a href="/wiki/Buccaneers" title="Buccaneers">buccaneer</a> <a href="/wiki/Clapp" title="Clapp">father</a> and losing a beloved <a href="/wiki/Ginny" title="Ginny">friend</a> to the whims of the World Nobles. Moreover, King <a href="/wiki/Bekori" title="Bekori">Bekori</a> of Sorbet, who enjoyed political support from the World Government, was frequently a thorn at Kuma's side, either through the use of smear campaigns or direct assaults towards Sorbet's more vulnerable population. Kuma became a revolutionary exactly to fight what he believed to be an unjust system propped up by hatred and corruption.
</p><p>In spite of his extremely antagonistic history with the World Government, the institution acknowledged Kuma's power and reputation as a pirate, which meant that they were willing to aid Kuma in his quest to save Bonney as long as he became their loyal tool as one of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a>. Because Vegapunk was the only person that could cure her and he worked for the World Government, Kuma had no choice but to submit himself to highly detrimental conditions that essentially stripped him of his own body, mind and soul, all so he could receive legal authorization for his daughter's surgical operation. Furthermore, Kuma was forbidden from ever meeting Bonney after the surgery's conclusion, under the threat of having her enslaved in that case. To further ensure Kuma's loyalty, Bonney was kept under the watch of <a href="/wiki/Cipher_Pol" title="Cipher Pol">Cipher Pol</a> agents during the final phases of her treatment, although the government at least honored Kuma's request to have the child returned to her homeland at Sorbet. Kuma also had a self-destructing mechanism installed within his body at Saturn's request, although Vegapunk had managed to secretly alter it to only shut down Kuma's vitals.
</p><p>The other Warlords generally had diverging opinions about Kuma. <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a> and <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a> both did not show interest on him, while <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a> did due to their shared status as <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">pirate</a> <a href="/wiki/Royal" title="Royal">royals</a>, a connection that was also not lost on <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a>. 
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">

  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">We have no obligation to cooperate with the Marines save where the government is directly involved... Your question shall remain unanswered.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
