<p><br>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Pacifista_Project.png/revision/latest?cb=20231226051931" class="image"><img alt="Pacifista Project" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pacifista Project.png" data-image-key="Pacifista_Project.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Pacifista_Project.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231226051931"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Pacifista_Project.png/revision/latest?cb=20231226051931" class="image"><img alt="Pacifista Project" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Pacifista_Project.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231226051931" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pacifista Project.png" data-image-key="Pacifista_Project.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Pacifista_Project.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231226051931"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pacifista_Project.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma unsettled with the Pacifista Project.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Prior to his final modifications, Kuma publicly claimed to follow the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>. However, he refused to cooperate with the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> unless given direct orders by his government superiors to do so. <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Moria</a> once stated that because of Kuma's perceived allegiance to the World Government, he worried him more than any other <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c474_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c474-6">[6]</a></sup> Kuma was also shown to have command over the Pacifista units during his visit to <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>, but did not seem to care about their presence, having no qualms in sending one away during the battle along with the rest of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>. After his <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> <a href="/wiki/Cyborg" class="mw-redirect" title="Cyborg">upgrades</a> were completed, Kuma became a slave to both the World Government and Marines alike, doing whatever he was commanded until his Revolutionary Army colleagues freed him. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Kuma_Restrained.png/revision/latest?cb=20230922020415" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Restrained" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma Restrained.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Restrained.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Kuma_Restrained.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230922020415"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Kuma_Restrained.png/revision/latest?cb=20230922020415" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Restrained" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Kuma_Restrained.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230922020415" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma Restrained.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Restrained.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Kuma_Restrained.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230922020415"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_Restrained.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma being restrained by Mary Geoise's security.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Between the abolition of the Seven Warlord system and his liberation from Mary Geoise, Kuma is now technically an enemy of the government once again despite his current mindless state. When Kuma returned to Mary Geoise by his own volition, the resident soldiers attempted to restrain him, with Kuma defending himself by causing major damage to the city. Sakazuki claimed that, since Kuma was no longer under the control of the government, he could no longer let the former Warlord to roam free and do as he pleased, and with the World Nobles further pressuring him, he had no other choice but to attempt to eliminate Kuma.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Borsalino">Borsalino</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kuma met <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a> four years ago at Vegapunk's lab, as the latter brought a fleet of marines to surround it due to orders from Saturn. The Admiral was present during the conversation regarding Kuma having to join the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a> and accept to become a human weapon for the government. Kizaru was visibly distraught on hearing Kuma agree to these terms as it would mean effectively losing all free will. As part of the deal, Kizaru stayed at Vegapunk's lab as Kuma and Bonney underwent their procedures, overseeing them. 
</p><p>For the following six months, Kuma and Kizaru grew close as they worked to build up Vegapunk's lab, partied and ate pizza alongside Bonney, Vegapunk and Sentomaru. After the procedures were done and Kuma's status as Warlord became official, however, their relationship grew sourer based on Kizaru's reaction to Kuma's presence on the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>. Upon seeing Kuma interfere with the PX-1 Unit, Kizaru questioned Kuma, who replied to the Admiral that his pact and loyalties were with the World Government and, as such, he did not have any obligation to explain his motives to the Marines. 
</p><p>Kuma and Kizaru became enemies the following two years after, with Kizaru deciding that with Kuma's presence on Egghead, he and his daughter needed to be eliminated, following Saturn's orders to kill them both.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Dr._Vegapunk">Dr. Vegapunk</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240512020453" class="image"><img alt="Kuma &amp; Vegapunk" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma &amp; Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240512020453"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240512020453" class="image"><img alt="Kuma &amp; Vegapunk" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240512020453" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma &amp; Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240512020453"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma and Vegapunk during an experiment.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kuma seems to have a good enough relationship with <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>, who always showed interest in Kuma's unique buccaneer physique. Vegapunk highly respects Kuma as a friend, as he modified the Warlord to be the prototype Pacifista while letting him act against the World Government's interests (like granting him his final wish as a human being, which was to program Kuma to protect the Straw Hats' ship until their return). 
</p><p>Kuma first learned about Vegapunk from Dragon, who had connections with the scientist since his <a href="/wiki/Freedom_Fighters" title="Freedom Fighters">Freedom Fighters</a> days and was responsible for directing Kuma himself to him. Because of this, Kuma came to fully trust Vegapunk despite his eccentricities and plans to improve the Marines' military strength, knowing that Dragon trusted him as well. Since Vegapunk was the man who saved Bonney's life, Kuma is immensely indebted to him. 
</p><p>That said, Bonney herself thought Vegapunk to be at fault for wiping away Kuma's mind. However, the truth was the opposite; Vegapunk was always against doing such a thing, considering it an inhumane act that the government had forced on him to carry out on Kuma. For this reason, Kuma's unexpected, but selfless acceptance of what was essentially a death sentence to himself shocked and moved Vegapunk to tears.
</p><p>Vegapunk has conducted several experiments on Kuma, including one where the latter was requested to materialize his memories through his own Devil Fruit abilities for Vegapunk to study. While Kuma at first refused, he eventually complied and allowed Vegapunk access to his now tangible memories. Vegapunk, out of respect, keeps Kuma's memories locked up inside a high-security room within his laboratory.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sentomaru">Sentomaru</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kuma met <a href="/wiki/Sentomaru" title="Sentomaru">Sentomaru</a> when he first visited Vegapunk at Egghead. Because Sentomaru would often (unwillingly) play with Bonney while Kuma talked with Vegapunk, he became friends with him as well. Sentomaru was also familiar enough with Kuma's Devil Fruit ability to have a gist about how it worked, despite treating some of its specific usages as rumors.
</p><p>Still, Sentomaru was always distrustful of Kuma because of his confusing allegiances and actions (especially in the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>), and occasionally addressed him as "Kuma-kou"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">くま公</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kuma-kō</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, an honorific meant as a sarcastic and insulting way of addressing someone. Despite this however he offered a silent prayer to Kuma when time came for Vegapunk to erase his memories and free will. Following the two years since the Summit War of Marineford, Sentomaru seemingly remained unaware of Kuma's intentions when the latter decided to protect the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a> through that time period thanks to a prior deal he had struck with Vegapunk, implying that he was kept in the dark about the scientist's involvement. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Nobles">World Nobles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As a child slave of the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a>, Kuma was endlessly abused and paraded around for his buccaneer strength. It was because of the nobles that Kuma lost both his parents, which filled him with despair. Kuma was considered a problematic, but still valuable slave, which was enough to force him into the <a href="/wiki/Native_Hunting_Competition" title="Native Hunting Competition">Native Hunting Competition</a> held at God Valley.
</p><p>Due to his current emotionless and inhuman state, he became a slave-to-rent for the World Nobles, as a punishment for him aiding the Straw Hat Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-3">[3]</a></sup> Seeing him unable to cry or scream regardless of injuries, the Celestial Dragons heavily abused him for their own pleasure, referring to him as a top-class slave until his eventual rescue. Due to his later arrival at Mary Geoise, where he damaged a good portion of the city and injured a few of them, many of the World Nobles ordered his execution by Sakazuki.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">[59]</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Jaygarcia_Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Saturn_Attacks_Young_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20240419013507" class="image"><img alt="Saturn Attacks Young Kuma" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="222" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Saturn Attacks Young Kuma.png" data-image-key="Saturn_Attacks_Young_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Saturn_Attacks_Young_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240419013507"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Saturn_Attacks_Young_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20240419013507" class="image"><img alt="Saturn Attacks Young Kuma" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Saturn_Attacks_Young_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240419013507" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="222" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Saturn Attacks Young Kuma.png" data-image-key="Saturn_Attacks_Young_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/76/Saturn_Attacks_Young_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240419013507"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Saturn_Attacks_Young_Kuma.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma being attacked by Saturn.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Jaygarcia_Saturn" title="Jaygarcia Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> can be best described as the 'devil' in Kuma's life, being largely responsible for most of the suffering Kuma has been forced to endure in his life. Kuma first met the elderly World Noble during the <a href="/wiki/God_Valley_Incident" title="God Valley Incident">God Valley Incident</a>, when he was merely nine years old. Saturn was seemingly already familiar with Kuma back then due to his <a href="/wiki/Buccaneers" title="Buccaneers">buccaneer</a> heritage and went on to confront the boy personally after he ate the <a href="/wiki/Nikyu_Nikyu_no_Mi" title="Nikyu Nikyu no Mi">Nikyu Nikyu no Mi</a>.
</p><p>According to Saturn, Kuma's enslavement is historically justified due to his race having committed an unknown crime long ago. Kuma, however, defied Saturn's way of thinking, declaring that no one can be born a slave and that he would model himself after the legendary <a href="/wiki/Nika" title="Nika">Nika</a>, saving the oppressed with the powers he had received. This response only reinforced Saturn's views that buccaneers had to be erased for good, telling Kuma his only options were to live as a slave or die.
</p><p>Years later, Saturn would start hearing about Kuma more frequently, as a revolutionary and as king of Sorbet. He also discovered the secret deal he tried to arrange with Vegapunk to save Bonney's life. Being against negotiating with pirates and spending Marine resources on saving a single girl, Saturn tried to make the most of this opportunity by having Kuma become a powerful tool for the government, enforcing several conditions he had to follow in order to ensure his obedience to the institution in the long term; including having his free will removed during his conversion into a Pacifista. Moreover, Saturn requested Vegapunk to implant a self-destruct system within Kuma's modifications in case they ever lost control of him, much to Vegapunk's protest.
</p><p>Despite having his free will removed, it appeared Kuma still retained key memories of his life and was aware of Saturn's presence on Egghead and that he was endangering his daughter. This led Kuma to retaliate after years of abuse and persecution and strike Saturn with a devastating punch.<sup id="cite_ref-c1104_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1104-60">[60]</a></sup> Saturn grew confused and furious at how this was possible and decided to kill Kuma with his own hands.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_2">Other</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gecko_Moria">Gecko Moria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a> feels that because of Kuma's apparent loyalty to the World Government, he could not be trusted and admitted that the Tyrant worried him more than any other Warlord. Moria also thought very little of Kuma's own Devil Fruit abilities back when the latter was accepted in the group, although he would later learn about their full potential somehow.
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Arc" title="Thriller Bark Arc">Thriller Bark Arc</a>, Kuma met with Moria to inform him about <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Marshall D. Teach</a>'s acceptance into the Seven Warlords of the Sea, and also warn him about the government's concerns that Moria could potentially lose against the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>. As such, Kuma offered his assistance to the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Pirates" title="Thriller Bark Pirates">Thriller Bark Pirates</a> in order to take down Luffy and his crew, but Moria, with his pride on the line, rejected this offer and even screamed back at Kuma for implying that he was not capable of doing the job himself.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marshall_D._Teach">Marshall D. Teach</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kuma has not met <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a> directly but showed to have prior knowledge of him before he was elected as a Warlord. Despite his unknown bounty, he knew about his past history as a member of the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a> and was opposed to his appointment, showing his doubts over the matter. Kuma's doubts would prove correct, as Blackbeard used his position as a Warlord to invade <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a> and recruit Level 6 prisoners to strengthen his crew.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bekori">Bekori</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Because of <a href="/wiki/Bekori" title="Bekori">Bekori</a>'s unfair policies that targeted the vulnerable elderly population of Sorbet, Kuma became an enemy of the Sorbet king. During an incident where some villagers that Kuma took care of were kidnapped by the kingdom's royal army, Kuma began a fight with the kidnapping soldiers and caused mass destruction to Sorbet's Castle Town, leading to his imprisonment as well as that of Ginny and some of Kuma's other friends who protested for his release. After Bekori's forceful dethronement by the <a href="/wiki/Freedom_Fighters" title="Freedom Fighters">Freedom Fighters</a>, Kuma joined the organization.
</p><p>Years later, when Bekori returned to Sorbet to continue with his atrocious policies, Kuma singlehandedly defeated the previously deposed king and his forces. This caused Bekori to seek direct support from the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>, starting a smear campaign against Kuma, the newly elected king of Sorbet. The propaganda directly attributed Bekori's own violent acts to Kuma's doing, while painting Bekori as an unfairly ousted leader who sought to recover his rightful nation.
</p><p>Kuma and Bekori met for the last time at sea, where the latter, with the support of a Marine fleet, attempted to kill the former and regain Sorbet's crown. Kuma, however, was able to take down the fleet with little trouble, stopping Bekori for good.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Tumi_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20240419001429" class="image"><img alt="Tumi Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tumi Infobox.png" data-image-key="Tumi_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Tumi_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240419001429"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Tumi_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20240419001429" class="image"><img alt="Tumi Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Tumi_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240419001429" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tumi Infobox.png" data-image-key="Tumi_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Tumi_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240419001429"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tumi_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma shows up by himself to liberate the country of Tumi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Prior to his final <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> modifications, Kuma was a soldier in the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a> and among its strongest and most effective fighters, as he could easily revert an unfavorable confrontation of national proportions by himself. As an officer-ranked fighter, he had control over its lower ranking members. However, he surrendered this control when he left the Revolutionary Army.
</p><p>As the former king of the <a href="/wiki/Sorbet_Kingdom" title="Sorbet Kingdom">Sorbet Kingdom</a>, he once held political power, however, Kuma himself only chose to rule due to popular demand, having no actual skill in governing a country, and as such gave much of his political power and responsibilities to one of the kingdom's previous rulers, <a href="/wiki/Bulldog" title="Bulldog">Bulldog</a>, effectively making himself a political figurehead. Nonetheless, the population still saw Kuma as their rightful ruler, and many citizens respected him as such, even after he returned to his life as a priest. When the previous ruler and tyrant, <a href="/wiki/Bekori" title="Bekori">Bekori</a>, returned in another attempt to take back the kingdom, Kuma fully abdicated from the throne and declared Bulldog as the official ruler, officially becoming a wanted pirate after confronting Bekori.
</p><p>During his days as a pirate, Kuma was considered a powerful and dangerous man, to the point of escaping and destroying entire marine fleets, stopping multiple bounty hunters, and gaining a fast-spreading reputation among other pirates as an unstoppable menace. His reputation became so well known that the World Government recognized him as a fitting candidate for the position as one of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a>, an offer that Kuma took as part of an agreement he made with <a href="/wiki/Jaygarcia_Saturn" title="Jaygarcia Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> to ensure Bonney's Sapphire Scales treatment. What made this even more impressive is the fact that Kuma achieved this reputation solo, without the assistance of a crew. This makes him, as well as fellow Warlord <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>, the only two known single-person pirate crews in the entire series.
</p><p>Kuma is one of the few people to have completely defeated the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> and is also the only character introduced so far that has defeated the crew single-handedly, twice. However, the crew was extremely weak and injured both times and they were in no shape to fight another battle, much less a Warlord (in the first encounter, the crew had just finished battling another Warlord of the Sea, <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>, as well as an island full of <a href="/wiki/Zombie" title="Zombie">zombies</a> and a giant zombie named <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Oars</a>; in the second encounter, they had just battled against a Pacifista while fending off a second, alongside <a href="/wiki/Sentomaru" title="Sentomaru">Sentomaru</a> and Marine <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a>). He did not want the crew dead, however, since he allowed them to escape, indicating he wasn't fighting them at full strength.
</p><p>Kuma has such a fierce reputation that even other powerful and famous pirates are unnerved by him, as seen when the captain of the <a href="/wiki/Kid_Pirates" title="Kid Pirates">Kid Pirates</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Eustass Kid</a>, seemed heavily disturbed when he witnessed the arrival of a Pacifista (mistaking it for the real Kuma) on the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a>, despite the fact that his bounty was higher than Kuma's former one.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kuma was born as a member of the extant <a href="/wiki/Buccaneers" title="Buccaneers">Buccaneers</a> race; a race said to carry the blood of <a href="/wiki/Giants" title="Giants">Giants</a> within them, having inherited his size and great physical strength and durability from his father <a href="/wiki/Clapp" title="Clapp">Clapp</a>; who was a full-blooded Buccaneer. Despite being only half-buccaneer on his father's side, Kuma has inherited the majority of the physical traits and abilities attributed to the Buccaneers, as he was incredibly strong even as a child, and withstood the harshest of punishments, beatings, and the overall lifestyle of enslavement by the Celestial Dragons even at such a young age. It is currently unknown how exactly durable and powerful Kuma's body was before he began the process of becoming a cyborg, but in his past, he was known to be quite fearsome even before becoming a revolutionary.
</p><p>After fully becoming a Pacifista, Kuma's physical abilities were enhanced further as a complete cyborg. He was able to protect the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a> from being damaged or touched by attackers for two entire years, and his body withstood two years' worth of damage as he waited for one of the Straw Hats to return. He could now take the harsh treatment and enslavement of the Celestial Dragons without feeling any pain at all, to the point where he could still move perfectly fine even after being stabbed with a multitude of swords and was visibly and heavily damaged and in need of repairs. This led to the Celestial Dragons identifying Kuma as their so-called "Invincible Slave".
</p><p>After being freed and repaired by the Revolutionaries, Kuma maintained enough strength and durability to send himself back to the Sabaody Archipelago, and then began climbing the Red Line itself to return to Mary Geoise, withstanding multiple onslaughts of attacks from the Marines. Despite the damage his body took just to successfully climb up to Mary Geoise, Kuma was more than strong enough to fight off Mary Geoise's guards, and even managed to devastate the whole area with his powers before Fleet Admiral Sakazuki finally showed up to stop him. Despite losing part of his face and one of his feet to him, Kuma was able to avoid capture and destruction, and escape before further damage was done.
</p><p>Once arriving to Egghead, he took a hit from Saturn's clawed foot while protecting Bonney, which while inflicting another grievous injury onto him, Kuma gathered enough strength to throw a very powerful Armament Haki-infused punch, sending the Elder crashing through several buildings and tearing off his arm and horn.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Geographical_Knowledge">Geographical Knowledge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kuma appears to have great knowledge in geography, as he knows exactly where he is sending someone through his powers, no matter in which part of the world he currently is. Part of this is due to his days traveling to a multitude of various islands searching for a cure for his daughter. His degree of spatial knowledge is high enough to perfectly locate even a moving sky island.
</p><p>Kuma is seemingly a skilled navigator as well, having travelled through a good portion of the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> by his sole self, while in a small boat.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Nikyu_Nikyu_no_Mi" title="Nikyu Nikyu no Mi">Nikyu Nikyu no Mi</a></i></dd></dl>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">

  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">If you were to go on a vacation... where would you like to go?</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>

<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Kuma before using his Devil Fruit powers.<sup id="cite_ref-c1473_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1473-61">[61]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>

<p><br>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c8/Kuma_Paw_Pads.png/revision/latest?cb=20230521133138" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Paw Pads" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma Paw Pads.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Paw_Pads.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c8/Kuma_Paw_Pads.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230521133138"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c8/Kuma_Paw_Pads.png/revision/latest?cb=20230521133138" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Paw Pads" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c8/Kuma_Paw_Pads.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230521133138" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma Paw Pads.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Paw_Pads.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c8/Kuma_Paw_Pads.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230521133138"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_Paw_Pads.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma reveals his Devil Fruit ability.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Thirty-eight years ago, Kuma ate the Nikyu Nikyu no Mi, a <a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that gave him paw pads on the palms of his hands; these paw pads have the power to repel anything they come into contact with. His paw pads grant him an absolute defense that allows him to protect himself from all physical attacks, even swords. This ability, coupled with his vast reaction speed, allows him to repel attacks from extremely quick opponents, such as <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> in <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_2_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 2 Techniques">Gear 2</a>. He can also use his paws to attack by repelling his target at great speed. By Kuma's own admission, his paw pads repel things at the speed of light.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e6/Tsuppari_Pad_Ho.png/revision/latest?cb=20230123013556" class="image"><img alt="Tsuppari Pad Ho" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tsuppari Pad Ho.png" data-image-key="Tsuppari_Pad_Ho.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e6/Tsuppari_Pad_Ho.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230123013556"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e6/Tsuppari_Pad_Ho.png/revision/latest?cb=20230123013556" class="image"><img alt="Tsuppari Pad Ho" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e6/Tsuppari_Pad_Ho.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230123013556" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tsuppari Pad Ho.png" data-image-key="Tsuppari_Pad_Ho.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e6/Tsuppari_Pad_Ho.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230123013556"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tsuppari_Pad_Ho.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma compressing air.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>His palm strikes are able to deal significant damage to his enemies, due his repelling power subjecting his target to a severe level of force. Additionally, his power to repel is not just strong, it is also focused into a cannon-like blast, enough to create a deep hole through thick stone. His paw strikes can also travel beyond the target, dealing identical damage to anything behind them as well. Kuma can even repel the air itself, attacking his opponent with a cannon-like shockwave. He can also compress an immense amount of air between his hands into a single small bubble, and then release the air bubble, which explodes as a super-massive shockwave that can decimate an entire island.
</p><p>Interestingly, he can repel all the pain, injury, and exhaustion out of a person's body, allowing him to completely heal people in an instant, even if they have suffered an incredibly severe level of damage. Once the pain is expelled from the person's body, it takes the form of a paw-shaped bubble, the greater damage that was removed, the larger the bubble will be. The damage can be transferred into another person's body, causing them a great deal of suffering all at once.
</p><p>Possibly the most impressive application of this fruit is that Kuma can send someone flying over vast distances, even across the world and traveling over the course of several days. The victim of this ability is encased in a paw bubble that protects them from and breaks through any obstacles that are in the way of the destination of Kuma's choosing. To an outside observer, the victim appears to vanish.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pacifista_Modifications">Pacifista Modifications</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Kuma%27s_Cybernetic_Enhancements.png/revision/latest?cb=20230216133232" class="image"><img alt="Kuma's Cybernetic Enhancements" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="216" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma's Cybernetic Enhancements.png" data-image-key="Kuma%27s_Cybernetic_Enhancements.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Kuma%27s_Cybernetic_Enhancements.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230216133232"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Kuma%27s_Cybernetic_Enhancements.png/revision/latest?cb=20230216133232" class="image"><img alt="Kuma's Cybernetic Enhancements" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Kuma%27s_Cybernetic_Enhancements.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230216133232" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="216" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma's Cybernetic Enhancements.png" data-image-key="Kuma%27s_Cybernetic_Enhancements.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Kuma%27s_Cybernetic_Enhancements.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230216133232"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma%27s_Cybernetic_Enhancements.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma's multiple cybernetic enhancements on his body,  exposed after being wounded by the Marines.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kuma is now a <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">cyborg</a> modified by <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>. He is, however, very different from other cyborgs, and displays strength and agility that are on a different scale.
</p><p>As with the other <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> models, Kuma has a built-in electronic recognition device within his pupils, which enables him to accurately identify certain individuals (presumably anybody that is listed within the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>'s bounty system) and their bounty count from across a distance of several dozen meters. Kuma is also equipped with augmented hearing, allowing him to pick up any sounds at a greater range than normal.
</p><p>Kuma's massive build along with his cybernetic enhancements grants him tremendous durability and strength comparable if not superior to other Pacifista; the average Pacifista model is capable of withstanding a combination assault from the pre-timeskip Monster Trio. At <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>, he effortlessly lifted a large slab of rubble with a single hand and his body was resilient enough to withstand most physical attacks, including <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s "Concasser" (in fact, Sanji injured his leg after delivering the blow, despite it being strong enough to stun a <a href="/wiki/Blueno" title="Blueno">user</a> of <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Tekkai" title="Rokushiki/Tekkai">Tekkai</a>) and even <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a>'s "Shishi Sonson", a technique that was able to cut through steel, which only left a scratch on Kuma despite it being a surprise attack.<sup id="cite_ref-c485_35-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c485-35">[35]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Emporio_Ivankov" title="Emporio Ivankov">Emporio Ivankov</a>'s "Galaxy Wink" appeared to inflict no substantial damage upon Kuma, despite the barrage of attacks being powerful enough to knock him off his feet.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Kuma_Fires_A_Laser_Beam.png/revision/latest?cb=20230124051021" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Fires A Laser Beam" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma Fires A Laser Beam.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Fires_A_Laser_Beam.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Kuma_Fires_A_Laser_Beam.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230124051021"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Kuma_Fires_A_Laser_Beam.png/revision/latest?cb=20230124051021" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Fires A Laser Beam" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Kuma_Fires_A_Laser_Beam.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230124051021" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma Fires A Laser Beam.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Fires_A_Laser_Beam.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Kuma_Fires_A_Laser_Beam.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230124051021"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_Fires_A_Laser_Beam.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma firing a laser beam from his mouth.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Even after two years of accumulated damage, lack of repair, and lack of sustenance intake, Kuma was still operational. While the modifications gave Kuma great strength, their full completion over a long time period apparently robbed Kuma of his free will.<sup id="cite_ref-PX-0_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PX-0-4">[4]</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to technically having his mind removed, Kuma does not feel any pain. While being enslaved by the World Nobles, Kuma was constantly and brutally abused by the World Nobles without feeling any discomfort, not even reacting as <a href="/wiki/Rosward" title="Rosward">Rosward</a> struck his head hard with a hammer and stabbed him with a sword. He has multiple swords stabbed inside his body and continues to function without succumbing to the accumulated damage.
</p><p>As a Pacifista, Kuma has the ability to shoot <a href="/wiki/Laser" title="Laser">laser</a> beams, which not only causes massive explosions upon detonation, but can also melt steel. This laser is apparently a replication of <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Pika_Pika_no_Mi" title="Pika Pika no Mi">Pika Pika no Mi</a> powers and for Kuma, this launcher is only installed in his mouth. In the other Pacifista, the launcher is installed on their palms as well. Kuma has his <a href="/wiki/Nikyu_Nikyu_no_Mi" title="Nikyu Nikyu no Mi">paw pads</a> instead of the laser holes on his hands; it is this aspect, along with the bible that only he holds, even after losing his free will, that distinguishes him from the other Pacifista, and makes him superior to them. However, he seems to possess gloves that allow him to shoot lasers from his palms, as he was about to demonstrate during <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Charlos</a>'s second attempt to kidnap <a href="/wiki/Shirahoshi" title="Shirahoshi">Shirahoshi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dc/Kuma_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20240122120104" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Armament Haki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="226" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma Armament Haki.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Armament_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dc/Kuma_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240122120104"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dc/Kuma_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20240122120104" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Armament Haki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dc/Kuma_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240122120104" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="226" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma Armament Haki.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Armament_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dc/Kuma_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240122120104"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_Armament_Haki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma hardening his fist.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kuma possesses the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a> and can utilize it to harden his fist, boosting the power of his punches.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup> With one Haki-infused punch, Kuma was able to knock <a href="/wiki/Jaygarcia_Saturn" title="Jaygarcia Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</a> off his feet and send him crashing into several buildings.<sup id="cite_ref-c1104_60-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1104-60">[60]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>He is also able to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vc2_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc2-66">[66]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ships">Ships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Kuma%27s_Ship.png/revision/latest?cb=20231211125410" class="image"><img alt="Kuma's Ship" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma's Ship.png" data-image-key="Kuma%27s_Ship.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Kuma%27s_Ship.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231211125410"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Kuma%27s_Ship.png/revision/latest?cb=20231211125410" class="image"><img alt="Kuma's Ship" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Kuma%27s_Ship.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231211125410" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma's Ship.png" data-image-key="Kuma%27s_Ship.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Kuma%27s_Ship.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20231211125410"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma%27s_Ship.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma's ship as a Warlord.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After becoming a pirate, Kuma had possession of at least three different ships. Initially, he had a rather small ship with two sails which barely had room to accommodate him. His subsequent ship was slighly larger, but only had one sail.<sup id="cite_ref-c1099_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1099-12">[12]</a></sup> Finally, after becoming a <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a>, he had a larger and more personalized ship with at least five sails, one at the front featuring his <a href="/wiki/Jolly_Roger" title="Jolly Roger">Jolly Roger</a> (based on a drawing from Bonney<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup>). The keel of the ship had a dot pattern similar to Kuma's hat and pants, the sides featured ornaments similar to his bear ears, and there was church-like structure on board with a cross at the top.<sup id="cite_ref-c1100p17_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1100p17-13">[13]</a></sup>
</p><p>He did not appear to have any crew aboard his ships at any point other than himself.<br style="clear:both;">
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Concepts">Early Concepts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ae/Early_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20150404102504" class="image"><img alt="Early Kuma" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="370" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Early Kuma.png" data-image-key="Early_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ae/Early_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150404102504"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ae/Early_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20150404102504" class="image"><img alt="Early Kuma" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ae/Early_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150404102504" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="370" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Early Kuma.png" data-image-key="Early_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ae/Early_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150404102504"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Early_Kuma.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuma's concept in One Piece Green.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In an interview about <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Film:_Strong_World" title="One Piece Film: Strong World">Strong World</a></i>, Oda revealed that he originally intended the steering wheel in the head concept of <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a> to be used on Kuma. He turned down the idea and decided later to use it for Shiki.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup>
</p><p>According to an interview in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Magazine_Vol.2" title="One Piece Magazine Vol.2">One Piece Magazine Vol.2</a>, Oda already intended for Kuma to separate the Straw Hats since his debut.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance_2">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the manga also, Kuma was intended to have a different color scheme than the one he is presented with in the anime. This unfortunately was because no full colored version of Kuma was present when the first episode of him appearing was made. The anime had Kuma with a black jacket while Oda's intentions were an orange one. The manga however later changed this color scheme to resemble that of the anime.<sup id="cite_ref-Kuma_True_Colors_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kuma_True_Colors-28">[28]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kuma_colors_2_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kuma_colors_2-29">[29]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kuma_colors_3_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kuma_colors_3-30">[30]</a></sup>
</p><p>In the manga and <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Unlimited_Cruise" title="One Piece: Unlimited Cruise">One Piece: Unlimited Cruise</a></i>, Kuma's paw pads are black, like a bear's. However, in the anime, the paw pads are pink, like a cat's (which may play off a concept in Robin's head of Kuma's Devil Fruit reminding her of a cat's pads).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Jaya_Arc">Jaya Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>During the meeting in Mary Geoise in the manga, Kuma had a few lines, but in the anime, he had none.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-War_Arc">Post-War Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the manga, during the flashback where Dragon saves the people of the Grey Terminal from a fire, Kuma's clothing underneath the common Revolutionary Army cloak was not shown. In the anime, it is revealed that Kuma had the same clothing then that he does now.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Arc">Dressrosa Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>During the flashback of Sabo's past, the anime shows Kuma being present in the training of Sabo where Kuma deflected Sabo after he tried to attack him.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D47&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><i>Kuma</i> means "bear" in Japanese, which represents his character's animal theme.</li>
<li>In the TV version of the Funimation dub of the anime, when Kuma is introduced, the word "BIBLE" is edited out of the book he is carrying. In the uncut DVDs, the word "BIBLE" is retained.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D48&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/One_Piece_POP_Bartholomew_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20150311020737" class="image"><img alt="One Piece POP Bartholomew Kuma" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="440" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="One Piece POP Bartholomew Kuma.png" data-image-key="One_Piece_POP_Bartholomew_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/One_Piece_POP_Bartholomew_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150311020737"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/One_Piece_POP_Bartholomew_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20150311020737" class="image"><img alt="One Piece POP Bartholomew Kuma" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/One_Piece_POP_Bartholomew_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150311020737" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="440" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="One Piece POP Bartholomew Kuma.png" data-image-key="One_Piece_POP_Bartholomew_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/One_Piece_POP_Bartholomew_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150311020737"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:One_Piece_POP_Bartholomew_Kuma.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">One Piece POP Bartholomew Kuma.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As a prominent character, he has appeared in the fan merchandise. Bartholomew Kuma has been featured with the Seven Warlords of the Sea in the series of <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Seven_Warlords_Cellphone_Strap" title="One Piece Seven Warlords Cellphone Strap">One Piece Seven Warlords Cellphone Strap</a> and twice in the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Super_Deformed_Figures" title="One Piece Super Deformed Figures">One Piece Super Deformed Figures</a>. Kuma has also been released in the P.O.P. <a href="/wiki/Portrait_of_Pirates" title="Portrait of Pirates">Portrait of Pirates</a> series. He was recently released in the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_DX_Figure" title="One Piece DX Figure">One Piece DX Figure</a> models. He was released in the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_World_Collectable_Figure" title="One Piece World Collectable Figure">One Piece World Collectable Figure</a> series in July 2010 along with the rest of the Seven Warlords and will be re-released in the same figure series (new ones are exactly the same but for a change in the color pattern of Doflamingo).
</p>
