<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FBartholomew_Kuma%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D54&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 122px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 122px; height: 122px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4a/Kuma%27s_Bible_Jaya.png/revision/latest?cb=20190712115043" class="image"><img alt="Kuma's Bible Jaya" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="75" height="100" data-image-name="Kuma's Bible Jaya.png" data-image-key="Kuma%27s_Bible_Jaya.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4a/Kuma%27s_Bible_Jaya.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/75?cb=20190712115043" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kuma's first bible in the Digitally Colored Manga during the <a href="/wiki/Jaya_Arc" title="Jaya Arc">Jaya Arc</a>.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 122px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 122px; height: 122px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Kuma%27s_Bible_Cover.png/revision/latest?cb=20190712115056" class="image"><img alt="Kuma's Bible Cover" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="88" height="100" data-image-name="Kuma's Bible Cover.png" data-image-key="Kuma%27s_Bible_Cover.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Kuma%27s_Bible_Cover.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/88?cb=20190712115056" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">The bible's cover in detail.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 122px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 122px; height: 122px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Kuma%27s_Bible_Back.png/revision/latest?cb=20190712115106" class="image"><img alt="Kuma's Bible Back" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="87" height="100" data-image-name="Kuma's Bible Back.png" data-image-key="Kuma%27s_Bible_Back.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Kuma%27s_Bible_Back.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/87?cb=20190712115106" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">The back of the bible.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 122px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 122px; height: 122px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/31/Kuma%27s_Bible_in_the_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest?cb=20190709103611" class="image"><img alt="Kuma's Bible in the Digitally Colored Manga" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="84" height="100" data-image-name="Kuma's Bible in the Digitally Colored Manga.png" data-image-key="Kuma%27s_Bible_in_the_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/31/Kuma%27s_Bible_in_the_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest?cb=20190709103611" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kuma's bible in the Digitally Colored Manga.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 122px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 122px; height: 122px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/25/Kuma%27s_Bible_Back_in_the_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest?cb=20190709103628" class="image"><img alt="Kuma's Bible Back in the Digitally Colored Manga" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="71" height="100" data-image-name="Kuma's Bible Back in the Digitally Colored Manga.png" data-image-key="Kuma%27s_Bible_Back_in_the_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/25/Kuma%27s_Bible_Back_in_the_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/71?cb=20190709103628" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">The back of the bible in the Digitally Colored Manga.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 122px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 122px; height: 122px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/04/Bartholomew_Kuma%27s_Bible_in_the_Summit_War_Saga.png/revision/latest?cb=20120921110628" class="image"><img alt="Bartholomew Kuma's Bible in the Summit War Saga" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="100" height="90" data-image-name="Bartholomew Kuma's Bible in the Summit War Saga.png" data-image-key="Bartholomew_Kuma%27s_Bible_in_the_Summit_War_Saga.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/04/Bartholomew_Kuma%27s_Bible_in_the_Summit_War_Saga.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20120921110628" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">The bible in the anime.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 122px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 122px; height: 122px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/31/Bartholomew_Kuma%27s_Bible_in_the_Thriller_Bark_Saga.png/revision/latest?cb=20190711142603" class="image"><img alt="Bartholomew Kuma's Bible in the Thriller Bark Saga" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="100" height="100" data-image-name="Bartholomew Kuma's Bible in the Thriller Bark Saga.png" data-image-key="Bartholomew_Kuma%27s_Bible_in_the_Thriller_Bark_Saga.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/31/Bartholomew_Kuma%27s_Bible_in_the_Thriller_Bark_Saga.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20190711142603" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kuma's bible in the <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Arc" title="Thriller Bark Arc">Thriller Bark Arc</a>.
</div></span></div>
<ul><li>Kuma's bible's design had changed over its appearances and media.
<ul><li>On the color spread and the digitally colored manga, the bible Kuma is carrying is gold-colored, with an orange title, and its back has the same pattern as Kuma's jacket. In the anime and games, the book is purple, and its back is not clearly seen.</li>
<li>On its <a href="/wiki/Chapter_233" title="Chapter 233">first appearance</a> during the Jaya Arc, the cover had a yellow figure over orange rays of light. In the anime, the figure is white and floating with yellow rays of light over a bluish-green background.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Chapter_234" title="Chapter 234">following chapter</a>, the back was shown to be blank, and the cover was clearly seen with the figure being that of a woman and the background features a skyline.</li>
<li>Starting with the end of the Thriller Bark Arc, the cover had a clearer image. In the colored version, the back cover is orange as the original coloring of Kuma's jacket. In the anime, this cover wasn't shown until the end of the <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago_Arc" title="Sabaody Archipelago Arc">Sabaody Archipelago Arc</a>. However, the figure is white, and the background is yellow.</li></ul></li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_3" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 3">One Piece: Pirate Warriors 3</a></i>, Kuma's bible is referred as <b>Book of Bears</b>.
<ul><li>Kuma's bible seemingly mentions the existence of <a href="/wiki/Sky_Island" title="Sky Island">Sky Islands</a>, as it was there that Bonney learned about them in the first place.</li></ul></li>
<li>Kuma's surname was most likely taken from the 18th century Welsh pirate <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bartholomew_Roberts" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bartholomew Roberts">"Black Bart" Bartholomew Roberts</a>.
<ul><li>Kuma was revealed to have been effectively dead during the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, which concluded the Golden Age of Pirates and began the "New Age". Coincidentally, it was Bartholomew Roberts whose death ended the real world's <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Golden_Age_of_Piracy" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Golden Age of Piracy">"Great Pirate Age"</a>.</li>
<li>Kuma may be named after <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bartholomew_the_Apostle" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bartholomew the Apostle">Bartholomew the Apostle</a>, one of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Apostles_in_the_New_Testament" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Apostles in the New Testament">twelve apostles of Jesus</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Kuma is the only known person to be affiliated with <a href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">pirates</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a>.</li>
<li>In the 4th, 5th, 6th, and 7th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan polls</a> of most popular characters, Kuma was ranked 52nd, 85th, 129th, and 98th, respectively, making him the least popular of the Seven Warlords both current and previous.</li>
<li>Kuma is the first <a href="/wiki/Cyborg" class="mw-redirect" title="Cyborg">cyborg</a> to appear in the series, though he was not revealed as one until the Thriller Bark Arc.</li>
<li>Kuma is one of the few cases in which his color scheme was displayed incorrectly in the anime and remained that way even after the official color scheme depicted by Oda was published. In fact, Oda replaced the original color scheme later with one similar in the anime.</li>
<li>Kuma's depiction as a child has similarities with a famous philosopher of the 19th century <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ninomiya_Sontoku" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ninomiya Sontoku">Ninomiya Sontoku</a>. Many statues portray him holding a book while he walks with a heavy load on his back.</li>
<li>Kuma is the only Warlord of the Sea known to be a parent.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card_-_One_Piece_Visual_Dictionary" title="Vivre Card - One Piece Visual Dictionary">Vivre Card databook</a>, Kuma's nickname of "Tyrant" was said to be given to him before joining the Revolutionary Army.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-3">[3]</a></sup> This contradicts <a href="/wiki/Chapter_1099" title="Chapter 1099">Chapter 1099</a> which takes place years after Kuma became a revolutionary, when Dragon says Kuma has recently been called "Tyrant".</li>
<li>Kuma's favorite foods are honey and salmon, both stereotypically associated with bears.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-3">[3]</a></sup></li></ul>
